# Comments for Question 4, LLM=Qwen 2.5 Max

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=6.2)
    The story attempts literary depth through symbolism (the bee pin as "both burden and beacon") and metaphor, but doesn't fully develop its thematic potential. The writing shows craft with evocative imagery and subtext, particularly in the final image of Clara's sketch mirroring the pin. However, the central conflict remains nebulous, and the story relies too heavily on telling rather than showing Clara's emotional journey. The ending gesture toward connection feels earned but incomplete.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=6.5)
    The story effectively uses the gelatinous substance as a metaphor for memories that cling and bind, creating emotional resonance. The central theme of forgiveness emerges organically from the narrative. However, the story relies too heavily on telling rather than showing the character's emotional journey, particularly in the final paragraphs. The ending insight about forgiveness feels somewhat rushed and declarative rather than earned through a more nuanced progression of the character's understanding.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=7.4)
    The story effectively uses symbolism, particularly the net representing connection across time and space. The writing style employs evocative imagery that enhances the otherworldly atmosphere. However, the emotional impact is somewhat muted by the abstract nature of Rhea's revelation and triumph. While there's a clear theme about facing fears and finding connection, the story would benefit from more concrete stakes or consequences to deepen its impact.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=7.4)

The central conflict between Elira and cosmic truth is well-established but remains entirely unresolved, leaving the impact somewhat diminished.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.5)

However, the conflict could be more clearly defined, and some emotional beats feel slightly rushed rather than fully developed within the word constraint.
